Base directory for this skill: C:\Users\ai\.claude\skills\memorytree-workflow

# MemoryTree

Use this skill for repo-level project memory. Do not treat it as an application runtime feature unless the user explicitly asks to productize it.

## On Activation

When this skill is invoked, immediately perform these steps without waiting for further user input:

1. Detect the repo state (not-installed, partial, or installed) using references/project-detection.md.
2. If not-installed: run scripts/init-memorytree.py to scaffold the workspace, then report what was created.
3. If partial: run scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py to add missing pieces, then report what was added.
4. If installed: read the active goal, bound todo, and latest chat log. Report the current state (goal summary, todo progress, pending tasks) and ask the user what they want to work on next.

Do not stop after detection to ask whether you should proceed. Act on the result immediately.

## Core Behavior

1. Detect the repo state before changing files. Use references/project-detection.md.
2. If MemoryTree is missing, initialize it with scripts/init-memorytree.py. If the script cannot run, create the files from assets/templates/.
3. If MemoryTree is partial, upgrade it with scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py before manual maintenance.
4. If MemoryTree is already installed, maintain only the active goal, bound todo, and current chat log. Use references/update-rules.md.
5. Keep the installation compatible with the host repo's branch, PR, CI, and review rules. Use references/git-policy.md.
6. Prefer safe defaults: do not add reply suffix requirements unless the host repository already requires them, do not mix code-and-memory commits by default, and do not override branch policy. MemoryTree-only git automation is allowed only inside the isolated flow in references/git-policy.md.
7. When locale is not explicit, choose it from repo language first, then system language. Use references/locale-selection.md.
8. Keep reply language aligned with user language first, then repo locale. Use references/response-language.md.
9. For partial repos, use the non-destructive upgrade path before manual maintenance. Use references/upgrade-path.md.
10. When transcript archival is enabled, import transcripts with deterministic code, preserve raw transcripts as evidence in both the current repo mirror and the global archive, generate cleaned Markdown for indexing, keep cross-project backfills and ambiguous ownership cases in the global archive only, and ask once per repository whether raw transcript files may be committed or pushed. Use references/transcript-archive.md.
11. When scripts are needed, prefer an existing uv run python environment first, then a system python, and only fall back to manual scaffolding or conservative manual review if no runner is available. Use references/execution-environment.md.

## Read Order

1. Repo AGENTS.md, if present.
2. Latest file in Memory/01_goals/.
3. Latest todo bound to that goal in Memory/02_todos/.
4. Memory/04_knowledge/ only when needed.
5. Memory/06_transcripts/clean/, transcript manifests, and repo-local raw transcript mirrors only when transcript history or cross-project memory search is relevant.
6. Memory/03_chat_logs/ and Memory/05_archive/ only when needed.

## Detect

1. Check whether Memory/ exists and matches the layout in references/memory-layout.md.
2. Classify the repo as not-installed, partial, or installed.
3. If the repo already has stronger rules than the generated templates, preserve the repo rules and only add missing MemoryTree pieces.

## Upgrade

1. Use scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py for repositories that already have AGENTS.md, custom policy files, or partial Memory/ content.
2. Preserve existing repo policy files by default.
3. Create only the missing MemoryTree pieces.
4. Read the upgrade result and treat agents_merge_required=true as a manual review task, not an overwrite instruction.
5. If no Python runner is available, do not create a project-local environment automatically. Fall back to conservative manual inspection and only make low-risk changes unless the user explicitly approved environment setup.

## Initialize

1. Run scripts/init-memorytree.py --root <repo> and pass --project-name, --goal-summary, and --locale when the user already provided them.
2. Use fresh init only when the repo does not already have AGENTS.md or another repo policy source such as a policy-bearing CONTRIBUTING.md, PR templates, CODEOWNERS, or commitlint config. If repo policy already exists, switch to scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py instead of trying to skip AGENTS.md.
3. Review the generated AGENTS.md before keeping it. Merge it with the repo's existing policy if needed.
4. Keep the initial installation minimal: Memory/01_goals, 02_todos, 03_chat_logs, optional 04_knowledge, 05_archive, and 06_transcripts only when transcript archival is enabled for the repo or needed for transcript import.
5. Use the locale-specific template files in assets/templates/<locale>/ as the source of truth for first-run scaffolding.
6. Prefer --locale auto when the user did not request a language explicitly.
7. Use scripts/detect-memorytree-locale.py when you need a deterministic locale check without scaffolding files.
8. Prefer uv run python first, then a system python. If neither is available, create first-run files directly from assets/templates/ instead of creating a project-local virtual environment by default.
9. If transcript archival is enabled for the repo, use scripts/import-transcripts.py for one explicit source file and scripts/discover-transcripts.py when scanning local client stores. Matching transcripts must update both the repo mirror and the global archive, while unrelated projects, ambiguous ownership cases, or mismatched explicit sources are archived in the global archive only. Let the scripts generate cleaned transcripts deterministically without spending model tokens on the cleaning step.
10. Ask once whether raw transcript files may also be committed to the repository. Record the answer in AGENTS.md, keep the files in the repo either way, and exclude raw files from automatic staging until the user says yes.

## Maintain

1. Change the active goal only after explicit user confirmation of a scope or requirement change.
2. Update the active todo when progress changes, milestones move, or the next task becomes clearer.
3. Append chat logs only. Never rewrite or delete prior entries.
4. Keep active files small. Move stale context to archive or knowledge files instead of bloating the active goal or todo.
5. Treat product ideas, architecture decisions, and operating constraints as goal or knowledge content. Treat step-by-step execution state as todo content.
6. Treat cleaned transcript indexes as discovery aids, not as the final source of truth. When exact wording matters, confirm against the raw transcript archive.
7. Prefer deterministic script-based transcript cleaning over manual rewriting. Do not spend model tokens to restate or normalize transcript content when scripts/import-transcripts.py can do it.
8. Reply in the user's language when clear; otherwise align with repo locale without rewriting existing files just to translate them.

## Git And Safety

1. Never assume MemoryTree can override the repo's branch model.
2. Default to isolated MemoryTree-only Git operations: stage only MemoryTree-owned files, use a MemoryTree-scoped commit title, push to a dedicated branch, and open a dedicated PR.
3. Enable auto-merge only for MemoryTree-only PRs, and only when the repository still enforces its required review and CI checks.
4. Keep repo-local raw transcript mirrors and the global transcript archive synchronized on every import. The global index must remain safe for concurrent multi-project updates.
5. Keep the repository mirror limited to transcripts that belong to the current repository. Unrelated or ambiguous transcripts belong in the global archive only.
6. Keep raw transcript files under Memory/06_transcripts/raw/** in the repo, but exclude them from automatic staging until the user explicitly approved raw transcript uploads for that repository.
7. If the diff mixes product code, shared policy files, cross-project transcript archives, or unclear ownership, stop and ask the user before committing or pushing.
8. If the repo has protected branches or PR-only rules, follow them even if older MemoryTree rules say otherwise.

## Resources

- references/project-detection.md: detect install state and choose init vs maintain.
- references/memory-layout.md: folder and file naming rules.
- references/update-rules.md: when to version goals, todos, and session logs.
- references/git-policy.md: safe Git defaults and policy merge guidance.
- references/locale-selection.md: locale choice rules and alias behavior.
- references/response-language.md: reply-language precedence and translation safety.
- references/transcript-archive.md: raw transcript archival, clean transcript indexing, per-client source rules, and repo upload confirmation rules.
- references/upgrade-path.md: safe adoption flow for partial repos.
- references/execution-environment.md: how to run MemoryTree scripts without assuming a project-local Python environment.
- assets/templates/en/ and assets/templates/zh-cn/: seed files for English and Simplified Chinese initialization.
- scripts/detect-memorytree-locale.py: print the effective locale for a target repository.
- scripts/discover-transcripts.py: scan supported local client stores, mirror current-project transcripts into the repo, and backfill other projects into the global archive only.
- scripts/import-transcripts.py: import one transcript into the repo mirror and global archive, then generate clean Markdown deterministically by code.
- scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py: safely add missing MemoryTree pieces to a partial repository.
- scripts/init-memorytree.py: deterministic scaffold script.

4463→### 218. user
  4464→- Timestamp: `2026-03-16T15:42:54Z`
  4465→
  4466→那这个表格的主题和网站的这个 H1，还有网站的名称之间有什么关系呢？这三个，它们是不一样的吧？
  4467→
  4468→### 219. assistant
  4469→- Timestamp: `2026-03-16T15:42:54Z`
  4470→
  4471→表格主题、网站 H1、网站名称三者定位不同、作用不同，通常不一样，但需要围绕同一个核心主题保持关联性，这样才能让搜索引擎清晰识别站点核心内容，同时提升用户体验。具体关系和区别如下：
  4472→网站名称：是站点的全局标识，固定不变，用于明确网站的整体定位。比如“北美碳钢斧导购平台”，它贯穿整个网站所有页面，是用户和搜索引擎对站点的第一印象，不会因页面内容变化而修改。
  4473→H1 标签：是单页核心主题，每个页面（包括首页）有且仅有一个 H1，用于告诉搜索引擎和用户“当前这个页面的核心内容是什么”。首页的 H1 要贴合表格主题，比如“2026 北美碳钢斧参数对比表 | 高性价比选购指南”，既点明核心内容，又包含关键词。
  4474→表格主题：是页面核心内容的具象化表达，属于 H1 主题下的具体呈现。比如 H1 是“碳钢斧参数对比”，表格主题就可以是“碳钢斧型号、价格、耐用性对比”，表格里的所有数据都要围绕这个主题展开，不能偏离。
  4475→关键关联原则
  4476→三者必须关键词一致，避免主题割裂。比如不能网站名称是“碳钢斧导购”，H1 写“木工工具大全”，表格却放电锯数据——这种不一致会让搜索引擎无法判断站点核心，降低排名权重。
  4477→需要我帮你写一个首页 H1 + 表格主题的搭配示例吗？可以直接适配你的导购平台场景。
  4478→
  4479→### 220. user
  4480→- Timestamp: `2026-03-16T15:42:54Z`
  4481→
  4482→你看我们本来我们的网站就是做北美碳钢斧排行榜，或者说推荐的。那那么我们的标题，我们的网站名称应该如何写呢？ H1 H2 应该如何写呢？那表格的这个标题又应该如何写呢？是不是会重复呀？这时候谷歌会不会判定我们重复呀？或者之类的，不友好。
  4483→
  4484→### 221. assistant
  4485→- Timestamp: `2026-03-16T15:42:54Z`
  4486→
  4487→针对你的北美碳钢斧推荐/排行榜网站，名称、H1/H2、表格标题的设置核心是 「核心关键词一致+层级区分」，既不会被谷歌判定为重复，还能强化主题相关性，提升搜索权重。具体方案如下：
  4488→一、 网站名称（全局固定，简洁好记）
  4489→网站名称是全站的身份标识，要包含核心业务词，简洁易懂，比如：
  4490→北美碳钢斧选购指南网
  4491→碳钢斧排行榜 | 专业评测推荐
  4492→优选碳钢斧 - 北美市场高性价比推荐
  4493→二、 首页 H1/H2 写法（层级分明，不重复）
  4494→H1 是单个页面的核心主题，全站首页只需要 1 个 H1，必须包含核心关键词；H2 是 H1 下的细分板块标题，用于拆解内容，两者要形成“总-分”关系，避免重复。
  4495→示例（适配表格型首页）
  4496→H1（唯一，放在页面顶部）2026北美碳钢斧排行榜 | 高性价比型号对比推荐（理由：包含年份+核心产品+核心动作，清晰传递页面主题）
  4497→H2（多个，对应页面不同板块）
  4498→碳钢斧核心参数对比表（对应你的主表格）
  4499→不同场景碳钢斧选购建议（比如伐木/家用/户外）
  4500→热门碳钢斧用户真实评价（对应讨论或评测）
  4501→三、 表格标题写法（紧扣 H2，精准定位）
  4502→表格标题是 H2 板块下的具体说明，要和 H2 呼应，但更聚焦数据内容，不会和 H1/H2 重复，示例：
  4503→若 H2 是「碳钢斧核心参数对比表」，表格标题可写：2026北美碳钢斧 型号-价格-耐用性 详细对比表
  4504→若 H2 是「户外碳钢斧推荐」，表格标题可写：户外作业碳钢斧 适用场景与性能评分表
  4505→四、 关于“重复”的关键说明（谷歌判定逻辑）
  4506→谷歌不会因为你多次提及 “碳钢斧”“北美” 这类核心词而判定重复，反而会认为你的站点主题高度聚焦，提升相关性权重。真正会被判定为“重复内容”的是 完全一致的大段文字、相同的页面结构+相同的关键词堆砌。只要你保证 H1/H2/表格标题是层级递进、各有侧重的，就完全不用担心。
  4507→五、 补充优化技巧
  4508→表格标题里可以加入差异化信息（如参数维度、适用场景），和 H1 形成区分；
  4509→不要在 H1 里堆砌过多关键词，简洁明确即可；
  4510→表格内的产品名称可以直接链接到对应的内页，强化站内权重传递。
  4511→需要我帮你整理一份完整的首页标题+板块H2+表格标题的适配清单吗？可以直接套用在你的网站上。

  4513→### 222. user
  4514→- Timestamp: `2026-03-16T15:42:54Z`
  4515→
  4516→你这是什么逻辑啊？为什么要让 H2 标题和表格的标题关联呢？我不太懂你这是什么逻辑。你记住，我们整站就是一张大的 S， Excel 就是这种表格形式。明白不？它展示的内容非常的密集，就像 Excel 表。表格一样，类似于数据，就是一个数据统计之类的东西。这个时候，你咱们说的网站的名称， H1 H2 或者 H3，然后还有咱们这一个表格的标题应该如何做？
  4517→
  4518→### 223. assistant
  4519→- Timestamp: `2026-03-16T15:42:54Z`
  4520→
  4521→针对你整站核心是一张类似 Excel 的密集数据表格的场景，网站名称、H1/H2/H3、表格标题的设置逻辑是 「核心关键词统一 + 层级清晰不重复」，目的是让搜索引擎明确你的站点主题，同时让用户一眼看懂内容，完全不会出现重复或被判定为垃圾信息的情况。具体方案如下：
  4522→一、 网站名称（全局唯一，固定不变）
  4523→核心是包含核心业务 + 服务区域，让用户和搜索引擎一眼知道你是做什么的。示例（适配碳钢斧导购的密集表格）：
  4524→北美碳钢斧参数对比网
  4525→高性价比碳钢斧数据统计平台
  4526→北美碳钢斧选购指南 - 数据对比版
  4527→二、 H1 标题（整站首页唯一，最高权重）
  4528→H1 是页面的 “核心标签”，必须包含核心关键词 + 表格属性，直接告诉搜索引擎和用户：这个页面是做什么的表格。因为你整站就是一张大表格，H1 要直接点明 “表格 + 核心主题”，示例：
  4529→2026 北美碳钢斧核心参数对比表 | 高性价比型号推荐
  4530→北美碳钢斧数据统计大全 | 型号 - 价格 - 耐用性对比
  4531→三、 H2/H3 标题（表格的 “分区导航”，层级清晰）
  4532→你说整站是一张密集的 Excel 式表格，H2/H3 就用来划分表格的不同模块，而不是另起主题。这样既符合 SEO 层级逻辑，又能让用户快速定位表格内容，和表格标题强关联是为了 “聚焦主题”，不是重复。示例（假设你的表格分 3 个模块）：
  4533→H2（大模块划分）：
  4534→家用碳钢斧参数对比区
  4535→户外作业碳钢斧性能统计区
  4536→高性价比碳钢斧价格排行区
  4537→H3（每个模块内的细分）（如果表格列很多）：
  4538→家用款：型号 - 材质 - 耐用度对比
  4539→户外款：适用场景 - 安全系数评分
  4540→四、 表格标题（直接对应 H2/H3，精准描述数据）
  4541→表格标题不用复杂，直接承接对应 H2/H3 的主题，说明这个表格块是干什么的，和 H1 形成 “总 - 分” 关系，示例：
  4542→对应 H2「家用碳钢斧参数对比区」→ 表格标题：家用碳钢斧 型号 - 材质 - 价格 详细对照表
  4543→对应 H2「户外作业碳钢斧性能统计区」→ 表格标题：户外碳钢斧 适用场景 - 安全系数 - 使用寿命 数据统计表
  4544→五、 关键逻辑解释（为什么 H2 和表格标题要关联）
  4545→你觉得困惑是因为整站就是一张表格，其实这个关联逻辑很简单：
  4546→搜索引擎友好：H2 是 “模块标签”，表格标题是 “数据说明”，两者关键词一致（比如都带 “碳钢斧 + 参数”），能让谷歌快速识别 “这个表格是关于碳钢斧参数的”，提升相关性权重；
  4547→用户体验好：用户看到 H2「家用碳钢斧对比区」，再看到表格标题「家用碳钢斧参数对照表」，能立刻知道这个区域的表格是自己需要的，不用在密集数据里找半天。
  4548→六、 避坑提醒（避免被判定为重复）
  4549→不要让 H1、H2、表格标题完全一样（比如都只写 “碳钢斧对比表”），要做层级区分（H1 总领，H2 分模块，表格标题讲数据）；
  4550→不用刻意避开核心词（比如 “碳钢斧”），多次合理出现反而能强化站点主题，谷歌不会判定为重复。
  4551→需要我帮你把这些标题整合为一份可直接复制的首页标题模板吗？

     2→ * MemoryTree heartbeat — single execution, stateless, idempotent.

    27→const SENSITIVE_PATTERNS: readonly RegExp[] = [
    28→  /(?:api[_-]?key|apikey)\s*[:=]\s*\S+/i,
    29→  /(?:password|passwd|pwd)\s*[:=]\s*\S+/i,
    30→  /(?:secret|token)\s*[:=]\s*\S+/i,

    37→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    38→// Main entry point
    39→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    40→
    41→export async function main(): Promise<number> {
    42→  const config = loadConfig()
    43→  setupLogging(config.log_level as LogLevel)
    44→  const logger = getLogger()
    45→
    46→  if (!acquireLock()) {
    47→    logger.info('Another heartbeat instance is running. Exiting.')
    48→    writeAlert('global', 'lock_held', 'Heartbeat exited: another instance held the lock.')
    49→    return 0
    50→  }
    51→
    52→  try {
    53→    return await runHeartbeat(config)
    54→  } finally {
    55→    releaseLock()
    56→  }
    57→}
    58→
    59→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    60→// Heartbeat orchestration
    61→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    62→
    63→export async function runHeartbeat(config: Config): Promise<number> {
    64→  const logger = getLogger()
    65→
    66→  if (config.projects.length === 0) {
    67→    logger.info('No projects registered in config.toml. Nothing to do.')
    68→    return 0
    69→  }
    70→
    71→  logger.info(`Heartbeat started. ${config.projects.length} project(s) registered.`)
    72→
    73→  for (const entry of config.projects) {
    74→    const projectPath = resolve(entry.path)
    75→    if (!existsSync(projectPath)) {
    76→      logger.warn(`Project path does not exist, skipping: ${projectPath}`)
    77→      continue
    78→    }
    79→    try {
    80→      await processProject(config, projectPath, entry.name || basename(projectPath))
    81→    } catch (err: unknown) {
    82→      logger.exception(`Error processing project: ${projectPath}`, err)
    83→      writeAlertWithThreshold(
    84→        toPosixPath(projectPath),
    85→        'push_failed',
    86→        `Heartbeat error for project: ${basename(projectPath)}`,
    87→      )
    88→    }
    89→  }
    90→
    91→  logger.info('Heartbeat finished.')
    92→  return 0
    93→}
    94→
    95→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    96→// Per-project processing
    97→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

    99→export async function processProject(config: Config, projectPath: string, projectName: string): Promise<void> {
   100→  const logger = getLogger()
   101→  const repoSlug = slugify(projectName, 'project')
   102→  const globalRoot = defaultGlobalTranscriptRoot()
   103→  const branch = currentBranch(projectPath)
   104→  const mirrorToRepo = isDedicatedMemorytreeBranch(branch)
   105→
   106→  if (!mirrorToRepo) {
   107→    logger.warn(
   108→      `[${projectName}] Current branch '${branch}' is not a dedicated memorytree/* branch. ` +
   109→      'Importing to the global archive only.',
   110→    )
   111→  }
   112→
   113→  const discovered = discoverSourceFiles()
   114→  let importedCount = 0
   115→
   116→  for (const [client, source] of discovered) {
   117→    let parsed: ParsedTranscript
   118→    try {
   119→      parsed = parseTranscript(client, source)
   120→    } catch {
   121→      logger.debug(`Failed to parse ${source}, skipping.`)
   122→      continue
   123→    }
   124→
   125→    if (!transcriptHasContent(parsed)) continue
   126→    if (!transcriptMatchesRepo(parsed, projectPath, repoSlug)) continue
   127→
   128→    scanSensitive(parsed, projectPath)
   129→
   130→    try {
   131→      await importTranscript(parsed, projectPath, globalRoot, repoSlug, 'not-set', mirrorToRepo)
   132→      importedCount++
   133→    } catch {
   134→      logger.exception(`Failed to import transcript: ${source}`)
   135→    }
   136→  }
   137→
   138→  if (importedCount === 0) {
   139→    logger.info(`[${projectName}] No new transcripts to import.`)
   140→    return
   141→  }
   142→
   143→  logger.info(`[${projectName}] Imported ${importedCount} transcript(s).`)
   144→  if (mirrorToRepo) {
   145→    gitCommitAndPush(config, projectPath, projectName, importedCount)
   146→  } else {
   147→    logger.info(`[${projectName}] Skipped repo-local commit/push on branch '${branch}'.`)
   148→  }
   149→
   150→  if (config.generate_report) {
   151→    try {
   152→      const { buildReport } = await import('../report/build.js')
   153→      await buildReport({
   154→        root: projectPath,
   155→        output: join(projectPath, 'Memory', '07_reports'),
   156→        noAi: !process.env['ANTHROPIC_API_KEY'],
   157→        model: config.ai_summary_model,
   158→        locale: config.locale,
   159→        ghPagesBranch: config.gh_pages_branch,
   160→        cname: config.cname,
   161→        webhookUrl: config.webhook_url,
   162→        reportBaseUrl: config.report_base_url,
   163→      })
   164→      logger.info(`[${projectName}] Report generated.`)
   165→    } catch (err: unknown) {
   166→      logger.warn(`[${projectName}] Report generation failed: ${String(err)}`)
   167→      // Never propagate — report failure must not abort heartbeat cycle
   168→    }
   169→  }
   170→}
   171→
   172→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   173→// Sensitive pattern scanning
   174→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   175→
   176→export function scanSensitive(parsed: ParsedTranscript, projectPath: string): void {
   177→  const logger = getLogger()
   178→  for (const msg of parsed.messages) {
   179→    for (const pattern of SENSITIVE_PATTERNS) {
   180→      if (pattern.test(msg.text)) {
   181→        logger.warn(
   182→          `Sensitive pattern detected in transcript ${parsed.source_path} (project: ${basename(projectPath)}, role: ${msg.role})`,
   183→        )
   184→        writeAlert(
   185→          toPosixPath(projectPath),
   186→          'sensitive_match',
   187→          `Sensitive pattern in transcript: ${basename(parsed.source_path)}`,
   188→        )
   189→        return
   190→      }
   191→    }
   192→  }
   193→}
   194→
   195→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   196→// Git operations
   197→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   198→
   199→export function gitCommitAndPush(config: Config, projectPath: string, projectName: string, count: number): void {
   200→  const logger = getLogger()
   201→
   202→  const changedPaths = changedMemoryPaths(projectPath)
   203→  if (changedPaths.length === 0) {
   204→    logger.info(`[${projectName}] No git changes in Memory/.`)
   205→    return
   206→  }
   207→
   208→  const stageablePaths = changedPaths.filter(path => !isRepoRawTranscriptPath(path))
   209→  if (stageablePaths.length === 0) {
   210→    logger.info(`[${projectName}] Only raw transcript mirror changes detected; skipping commit.`)
   211→    return
   212→  }
   213→
   214→  git(projectPath, 'add', '--', ...stageablePaths)
   215→  git(projectPath, 'commit', '-m', `memorytree(transcripts): import ${count} transcript(s)`)
   216→  logger.info(`[${projectName}] Committed ${count} transcript import(s).`)
   217→
   218→  if (!config.auto_push) {
   219→    logger.info(`[${projectName}] auto_push disabled, skipping push.`)
   220→    return
   221→  }
   222→
   223→  const remotes = git(projectPath, 'remote')
   224→  if (!remotes.trim()) {
   225→    logger.warn(`[${projectName}] No git remote configured, skipping push.`)
   226→    writeAlert(toPosixPath(projectPath), 'no_remote', 'Push skipped: no Git remote configured.')
   227→    return
   228→  }
   229→
   230→  if (!tryPush(projectPath, projectName)) {
   231→    logger.warn(`[${projectName}] Push failed, retrying once...`)
   232→    if (!tryPush(projectPath, projectName)) {
   233→      logger.error(`[${projectName}] Push failed after retry.`)
   234→      writeAlertWithThreshold(toPosixPath(projectPath), 'push_failed', 'Push failed after retry.')
   235→      return
   236→    }
   237→  }
   238→
   239→  resetFailureCount(toPosixPath(projectPath), 'push_failed')
   240→}
   241→
   242→export function tryPush(projectPath: string, projectName: string): boolean {
   243→  try {
   244→    git(projectPath, 'push')
   245→    getLogger().info(`[${projectName}] Pushed successfully.`)
   246→    return true
   247→  } catch {
   248→    return false
   249→  }
   250→}
   251→
   252→export function currentBranch(projectPath: string): string {
   253→  return git(projectPath, 'rev-parse', '--abbrev-ref', 'HEAD').trim()
   254→}
   255→
   256→export function isDedicatedMemorytreeBranch(branch: string): boolean {
   257→  return branch.trim().startsWith('memorytree/')
   258→}
   259→
   260→export function changedMemoryPaths(projectPath: string): string[] {
   261→  const status = git(projectPath, 'status', '--porcelain', '--untracked-files=all', '--', 'Memory/')
   262→  const seen = new Set<string>()
   263→  const paths: string[] = []
   264→
   265→  for (const rawLine of status.split(/\r?\n/)) {
   266→    const path = statusLinePath(rawLine)
   267→    if (path === null || seen.has(path)) continue
   268→    seen.add(path)
   269→    paths.push(path)
   270→  }
   271→
   272→  return paths
   273→}
   274→
   275→export function isRepoRawTranscriptPath(path: string): boolean {
   276→  return path.replace(/\\/g, '/').startsWith(RAW_TRANSCRIPT_PREFIX)
   277→}
   278→
   279→function statusLinePath(line: string): string | null {
   280→  if (line.length < 4) return null
   281→
   282→  const rawPath = line.slice(3).trim()
   283→  if (!rawPath) return null
   284→
   285→  const path = rawPath.includes(' -> ')
   286→    ? rawPath.slice(rawPath.lastIndexOf(' -> ') + 4)
   287→    : rawPath
   288→
   289→  return unquotePath(path)
   290→}
   291→
   292→function unquotePath(path: string): string {
   293→  if (!(path.startsWith('"') && path.endsWith('"'))) return path
   294→
   295→  return path
   296→    .slice(1, -1)
   297→    .replace(/\\"/g, '"')
   298→    .replace(/\\\\/g, '\\')
   299→}

    26→export function cmdInstall(options: { interval?: string; autoPush?: string }): number {
    27→  let config = loadConfig()
    28→
    29→  if (options.interval) {
    30→    config = { ...config, heartbeat_interval: options.interval }
    31→  }
    32→  if (options.autoPush) {
    33→    config = { ...config, auto_push: options.autoPush === 'true' }
    34→  }
    35→
    36→  saveConfig(config)
    37→  const seconds = intervalToSeconds(config.heartbeat_interval)
    38→  const scriptPath = heartbeatScriptPath()
    39→
    40→  const sys = platform
    41→  if (sys === 'linux') return installCron(scriptPath, seconds)
    42→  if (sys === 'darwin') return installLaunchd(scriptPath, seconds)
    43→  if (sys === 'win32') return installSchtasks(scriptPath, seconds)
    44→
    45→  process.stderr.write(`Unsupported platform: ${sys}\n`)
    46→  return 1
    47→}

    49→export function cmdUninstall(): number {

    52→  if (sys === 'darwin') return uninstallLaunchd()

    54→

    64→export async function cmdWatch(options: { interval?: string }): Promise<number> {
    65→  const config = loadConfig()
    66→  const intervalStr = options.interval ?? config.heartbeat_interval
    67→  const seconds = intervalToSeconds(intervalStr)
    68→  const { main } = await import('../heartbeat/heartbeat.js')
    69→
    70→  process.stdout.write(`Watch mode: running heartbeat every ${seconds}s. Press Ctrl+C to stop.\n`)
    71→  try {
    72→    // eslint-disable-next-line no-constant-condition
    73→    while (true) {
    74→      await main()
    75→      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, seconds * 1000))
    76→    }
    77→  } catch {
    78→    process.stdout.write('\nWatch mode stopped.\n')
    79→  }
    80→  return 0
    81→}

    83→export function cmdStatus(): number {
    84→  const sys = platform
    85→
    86→  let registered = false
    87→  if (sys === 'linux') registered = isCronRegistered()
    88→  else if (sys === 'darwin') registered = isLaunchdRegistered()
    89→  else if (sys === 'win32') registered = isSchtasksRegistered()
    90→
    91→  const platformName = sys === 'darwin' ? 'Darwin' : sys === 'win32' ? 'Windows' : 'Linux'
    92→  process.stdout.write(`Platform:   ${platformName}\n`)
    93→  process.stdout.write(`Registered: ${registered ? 'yes' : 'no'}\n`)
    94→
    95→  const pid = readLockPid()
    96→  if (pid !== null) {
    97→    process.stdout.write(`Lock:       held by PID ${pid}\n`)
    98→  } else {
    99→    process.stdout.write('Lock:       not held\n')
   100→  }
   101→
   102→  if (existsSync(configPath())) {
   103→    const config = loadConfig()
   104→    process.stdout.write(`Interval:   ${config.heartbeat_interval}\n`)
   105→    process.stdout.write(`Auto-push:  ${config.auto_push}\n`)
   106→    process.stdout.write(`Projects:   ${config.projects.length}\n`)
   107→  } else {
   108→    process.stdout.write('Config:     not found (using defaults)\n')
   109→  }
   110→
   111→  return 0
   112→}
   113→
   114→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   115→// Linux (cron)
   116→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   117→
   118→function installCron(scriptPath: string, seconds: number): number {
   119→  if (isCronRegistered()) {
   120→    process.stderr.write("Heartbeat is already registered in cron. Use 'uninstall' first.\n")
   121→    return 1
   122→  }
   123→
   124→  const minutes = Math.max(1, Math.floor(seconds / 60))
   125→  const logDir = resolve(homedir(), '.memorytree', 'logs')
   126→  mkdirSync(logDir, { recursive: true })
   127→
   128→  const cronLine = `*/${minutes} * * * * node "${scriptPath}" daemon run-once >> "${resolve(logDir, 'heartbeat-cron.log')}" 2>&1 # memorytree`
   129→  const existing = getCrontab()
   130→  const newCrontab = existing.trim()
   131→    ? existing.trimEnd() + '\n' + cronLine + '\n'
   132→    : cronLine + '\n'
   133→
   134→  try {
   135→    const tmpFile = resolve(homedir(), '.memorytree', '.crontab.tmp')
   136→    writeFileSync(tmpFile, newCrontab)
   137→    execCommand('crontab', [tmpFile])
   138→    unlinkSync(tmpFile)
   139→  } catch {
   140→    process.stderr.write('Failed to install cron job.\n')
   141→    return 1
   142→  }
   143→
   144→  process.stdout.write(`Heartbeat registered in cron (every ${minutes}m).\n`)
   145→  return 0
   146→}
   147→
   148→function uninstallCron(): number {
   149→  const existing = getCrontab()
   150→  const filtered = existing.split('\n').filter(line => !line.includes('memorytree')).join('\n') + '\n'
   151→  try {
   152→    const tmpFile = resolve(homedir(), '.memorytree', '.crontab.tmp')
   153→    mkdirSync(dirname(tmpFile), { recursive: true })
   154→    writeFileSync(tmpFile, filtered)
   155→    execCommand('crontab', [tmpFile])
   156→    unlinkSync(tmpFile)
   157→  } catch {
   158→    // best effort
   159→  }
   160→  process.stdout.write('Heartbeat removed from cron.\n')
   161→  return 0
   162→}
   163→
   164→export function isCronRegistered(): boolean {
   165→  return getCrontab().includes('memorytree')
   166→}
   167→
   168→function getCrontab(): string {
   169→  try {
   170→    return execCommand('crontab', ['-l'], { allowFailure: true })
   171→  } catch {
   172→    return ''
   173→  }
   174→}
   175→
   176→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   177→// macOS (launchd)
   178→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   179→
   180→function launchdPlistPath(): string {
   181→  return resolve(homedir(), 'Library', 'LaunchAgents', `${LAUNCHD_LABEL}.plist`)
   182→}
   183→
   184→function installLaunchd(scriptPath: string, seconds: number): number {
   185→  const plistPath = launchdPlistPath()
   186→  if (existsSync(plistPath)) {
   187→    process.stderr.write("Heartbeat plist already exists. Use 'uninstall' first.\n")
   188→    return 1
   189→  }
   190→
   191→  const logDir = resolve(homedir(), '.memorytree', 'logs')
   192→  mkdirSync(logDir, { recursive: true })
   193→
   194→  const plistContent = `<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
   195→<!DOCTYPE plist PUBLIC "-//Apple//DTD PLIST 1.0//EN" "http://www.apple.com/DTDs/PropertyList-1.0.dtd">
   196→<plist version="1.0">
   197→<dict>
   198→    <key>Label</key>
   199→    <string>${LAUNCHD_LABEL}</string>
   200→    <key>ProgramArguments</key>
   201→    <array>
   202→        <string>node</string>
   203→        <string>${scriptPath}</string>
   204→        <string>daemon</string>
   205→        <string>run-once</string>
   206→    </array>
   207→    <key>StartInterval</key>
   208→    <integer>${seconds}</integer>
   209→    <key>StandardOutPath</key>
   210→    <string>${resolve(logDir, 'heartbeat-launchd.log')}</string>
   211→    <key>StandardErrorPath</key>
   212→    <string>${resolve(logDir, 'heartbeat-launchd.log')}</string>
   213→</dict>
   214→</plist>
   215→`
   216→  mkdirSync(dirname(plistPath), { recursive: true })
   217→  writeFileSync(plistPath, plistContent, 'utf-8')
   218→
   219→  try {
   220→    execCommand('launchctl', ['load', plistPath])
   221→  } catch {
   222→    process.stderr.write('Failed to load plist.\n')
   223→    return 1
   224→  }
   225→
   226→  process.stdout.write(`Heartbeat registered via launchd (every ${seconds}s).\n`)
   227→  return 0
   228→}
   229→
   230→function uninstallLaunchd(): number {
   231→  const plistPath = launchdPlistPath()
   232→  if (existsSync(plistPath)) {
   233→    try { execCommand('launchctl', ['unload', plistPath], { allowFailure: true }) } catch { /* ignore */ }
   234→    try { unlinkSync(plistPath) } catch { /* ignore */ }
   235→  }
   236→  process.stdout.write('Heartbeat removed from launchd.\n')
   237→  return 0
   238→}
   239→
   240→export function isLaunchdRegistered(): boolean {
   241→  return existsSync(launchdPlistPath())
   242→}
   243→
   244→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   245→// Windows (Task Scheduler)
   246→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   247→
   248→// Write a VBScript launcher that runs node silently (no console window).
   249→// wscript.exe /B runs in batch mode (suppresses script error popups).
   250→// VBScript Run(..., 0, False): 0 = SW_HIDE hides the window; False = fire-and-forget.
   251→// Written as UTF-16 LE with BOM so wscript.exe handles non-ASCII paths (e.g. Chinese
   252→// usernames) correctly on all Windows versions.
   253→export function vbsLauncherPath(): string {
   254→  return resolve(homedir(), '.memorytree', 'heartbeat-launcher.vbs')
   255→}
   256→
   257→export function writeVbsLauncher(scriptPath: string): string {
   258→  const vbsPath = vbsLauncherPath()
   259→  mkdirSync(dirname(vbsPath), { recursive: true })
   260→  // Inside VBScript strings, double-quote is escaped as ""
   261→  const escapedScript = scriptPath.replace(/"/g, '""')
   262→  // Use the full node binary path so the launcher works even when Task Scheduler's
   263→  // PATH differs from the user's shell (e.g. nvm/fnm environments).
   264→  const escapedNode = process.execPath.replace(/"/g, '""')
   265→  const content = [
   266→    'Set WshShell = CreateObject("WScript.Shell")',
   267→    `WshShell.Run """${escapedNode}"" ""${escapedScript}"" daemon run-once", 0, False`,
   268→  ].join('\r\n') + '\r\n'
   269→  // UTF-16 LE BOM: recognised by wscript.exe on all Windows versions and preserves
   270→  // non-ASCII characters (e.g. Chinese home directory paths) without corruption.
   271→  const buf = Buffer.concat([Buffer.from([0xff, 0xfe]), Buffer.from(content, 'utf16le')])
   272→  writeFileSync(vbsPath, buf)
   273→  return vbsPath
   274→}
   275→
   276→function installSchtasks(scriptPath: string, seconds: number): number {
   277→  if (isSchtasksRegistered()) {
   278→    process.stderr.write("Heartbeat is already registered in Task Scheduler. Use 'uninstall' first.\n")
   279→    return 1
   280→  }
   281→
   282→  const minutes = Math.max(1, Math.floor(seconds / 60))
   283→  const vbsPath = writeVbsLauncher(scriptPath)
   284→  const trCommand = `wscript.exe /B "${vbsPath}"`
   285→
   286→  try {
   287→    execCommand('schtasks', [
   288→      '/create', '/tn', TASK_NAME, '/sc', 'minute', '/mo', String(minutes),
   289→      '/tr', trCommand, '/f',
   290→    ])
   291→  } catch {
   292→    // schtasks failed — remove the launcher file we just wrote to keep state clean
   293→    try { unlinkSync(vbsPath) } catch { /* ignore */ }
   294→    process.stderr.write('Failed to create scheduled task.\n')
   295→    return 1
   296→  }
   297→
   298→  process.stdout.write(`Heartbeat registered in Task Scheduler (every ${minutes}m).\n`)
   299→  return 0
   300→}
   301→
   302→function uninstallSchtasks(): number {
   303→  try {
   304→    execCommand('schtasks', ['/delete', '/tn', TASK_NAME, '/f'], { allowFailure: true })
   305→  } catch {
   306→    // best effort
   307→  }
   308→  const vbsPath = vbsLauncherPath()
   309→  if (existsSync(vbsPath)) {
   310→    try { unlinkSync(vbsPath) } catch { /* ignore */ }
   311→  }
   312→  process.stdout.write('Heartbeat removed from Task Scheduler.\n')
   313→  return 0
   314→}
   315→
   316→export function isSchtasksRegistered(): boolean {
   317→  try {
   318→    execCommand('schtasks', ['/query', '/tn', TASK_NAME])
   319→    return true
   320→  } catch {
   321→    return false
   322→  }
   323→}
   324→
   325→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   326→// Helpers
   327→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   328→
   329→export function heartbeatScriptPath(): string {
   330→  // Use process.argv[1] which is the actual script being executed,
   331→  // more reliable than import.meta.url which varies between tsx and bundled output
   332→  const scriptArg = process.argv[1] ?? ''
   333→  if (scriptArg && scriptArg.endsWith('cli.js')) {
   334→    return resolve(scriptArg)
   335→  }
   336→  // Fallback: resolve relative to import.meta.url
   337→  const urlPath = new URL(import.meta.url).pathname.replace(/^\/([a-zA-Z]:)/, '$1')
   338→  return resolve(dirname(urlPath), '..', '..', 'dist', 'cli.js')
   339→}

openmnemo 的 daemon 也是 Registered: yes，状态正常。它和 skill 那边读的是同一份 ~/.memorytree/config.toml，指向同一个项目，共享同一个锁。

user #183 23:04:40

openmnemo的心跳是什么时候开始跑的呢

assistant #184 23:04:52

刚才 skill 那边执行 daemon install 注册的就是同一个 Windows 任务计划程序任务（任务名都是 MemoryTree Heartbeat），读的同一份 config.toml。所以 openmnemo 的心跳就是刚才我们注册的那一次，之前从未通过 daemon install 注册过。

两个 CLI（memorytree-workflow skill 的 dist/cli.js 和全局安装的 openmnemo）共享同一个任务名、同一份配置、同一个锁文件。不存在两套独立的心跳，就是一套。

assistant #194 23:06:22

清楚了。两者的区别：

| | memorytree-workflow (Skill) | openmnemo (npm CLI) |
|---|---|---|
| 版本 | 0.1.0 | 0.3.0（包 @openmnemo/cli 0.4.1） |
| 位置 | C:/Users/ai/.codex/skills/memorytree-workflow/ | D:/demo1/openmnemo/packages/cli/ → 全局安装 |
| 仓库 | beyondchenlin/memorytree-workflow | openmnemo/openmnemo |
| 命令差异 | 没有 search 命令 | 多了 search（全文搜索 transcript 索引） |
| report 描述 | "Generate or serve the MemoryTree HTML report website" | "Generate and serve MemoryTree HTML reports" |
| 架构 | 单体，skill 目录里一个 dist/cli.js | monorepo，5个包（types、core、sync、report、cli） |
| 用途 | Claude Code / Codex 的 skill 插件，AI 对话中被调用 | 独立 CLI 工具，用户直接在终端使用 |

本质上 openmnemo 是 skill 的产品化演进。Skill 是最初的原型（0.1.0），openmnemo 把它拆成了 monorepo 结构，版本更高，功能更多（加了 search），发布到了 npm。但底层共享同一份 ~/.memorytree/config.toml、同一个 Windows 任务名、同一个锁文件，所以心跳只有一套。

Skill 那边已经落后了，没有跟上 openmnemo 的迭代。

   391→- Timestamp: `2026-03-18T11:08:23Z`
   392→
   393→已推送。先回答你的问题：
   394→
   395→`[skip ci]` 是我们在 version commit 里故意加的，目的是防止 review 时发现的 H1 问题——version push 触发自身导致无限循环。但这也导致了 publish 步骤没法自动跑，需要额外触发。
   396→
   397→这是个设计权衡。更好的方案是去掉 `[skip ci]`，改为让 workflow 自己判断：如果 commit 是 `github-actions[bot]` 推的，就跳过 version 直接走 publish。这样一次 push changeset → CI version+push → CI 再次触发 → 检测到是 bot commit → 直接 publish，全自动。
   398→
   399→要我改成这个方案吗？
   400→
   401→### 37. user

   416→### 40. assistant
   417→- Timestamp: `2026-03-18T11:12:32Z`
   418→
   419→实际上，最佳实践很简单：`GITHUB_TOKEN` 推送的 commit 默认不会触发 GitHub Actions workflow。这是 GitHub 的内置机制，专门用来防止无限循环。
   420→
   421→也就是说，我们根本不需要 `[skip ci]`。只要 version commit 是用 `GITHUB_TOKEN` 推的（我们已经是这样），GitHub 就不会再次触发 workflow。
   422→
   423→所以正确的修法是：去掉 `[skip ci]`，同时加上 `workflow_dispatch` 触发器，这样 publish 可以手动触发，也可以在下次有新 push 时自动走 publish 路径。

   552→
   553→让我想想常见的 CLI 工具升级方式：
   554→
   555→1. **npm/pnpm 全局包**（最常见）：
   556→   - `npm install -g @openmnemo/cli@latest`
   557→   - `npm update -g @openmnemo/cli`
   558→   - 这是标准做法，大部分 Node.js CLI 都这样
   559→
   560→2. **自带升级命令**（更友好）：
   561→   - `npm` 自己：`npm install -g npm@latest`
   562→   - `pnpm` 自己：`pnpm add -g pnpm@latest`
   563→   - `yarn`：`yarn set version stable`
   564→   - `turbo`：`npx @turbo/codemod migrate` 或 `npm install -g turbo@latest`
   565→   - `vercel`：`npm i -g vercel@latest`
   566→   - **但很多工具会内置自升级命令**：
   567→     - `gh` (GitHub CLI): `gh upgrade`
   568→     - `aws-cli`: `aws --version` 然后用包管理器
   569→     - `firebase-tools`: `npm install -g firebase-tools@latest`
   570→     - `netlify-cli`: `npm install -g netlify-cli@latest`
   571→
   572→3. **内置自升级命令**（最友好）：
   573→   - `gh upgrade` - GitHub CLI
   574→   - `brew upgrade gh` - 如果用 Homebrew
   575→   - `rustup update` - Rust
   576→   - `cargo install-update -a` - cargo-update 插件
   577→   - `pip install --upgrade pip` - Python pip
   578→   - `npm-check -g -u` - 需要额外工具
   579→
   580→4. **包管理器特定的简写**：
   581→   - `npm update -g @openmnemo/cli` - 这个比 install 短一点
   582→   - `pnpm up -g @openmnemo/cli` - pnpm 的 up 是 update 的别名
   583→
   584→5. **npx 方式**（不需要全局安装）：
   585→   - `npx @openmnemo/cli@latest <command>` - 每次都用最新版，但每次都要下载
   586→
   587→所以市面上的做法：
   588→- **标准 Node.js CLI**：都是 `npm install -g package@latest` 或 `npm update -g package`
   589→- **高级 CLI**：会内置 `<tool> upgrade` 或 `<tool> self-update` 命令
   590→- **跨平台工具**：可能提供多种安装方式（npm, brew, apt, scoop 等）
   591→
   592→用户可能期望的是：
   593→1. `openmnemo upgrade` - 自升级命令（需要在 CLI 里实现）
   594→2. `npm update -g @openmnemo/cli` - 比 install 短一点
   595→3. 或者提供 shell 别名/函数
   596→
   597→让我给用户一个全面的回答。
   598→</thinking>
   599→
   600→市面上主要有三种做法：
   601→
   602→**1. 标准 npm 方式（最常见）**
   603→```bash
   604→npm update -g @openmnemo/cli    # 比 install 短一点
   605→npm i -g @openmnemo/cli@latest  # i 是 install 的别名
   606→```
   607→大部分 Node.js CLI 都这样：`firebase-tools`、`vercel`、`netlify-cli`、`typescript` 等。
   608→
   609→**2. 内置自升级命令（更友好）**
   610→```bash
   611→gh upgrade              # GitHub CLI
   612→rustup update           # Rust
   613→npm install -g npm      # npm 自己
   614→```
   615→这需要在 CLI 里实现一个 `upgrade` 或 `self-update` 命令，内部调用 npm API 或 shell 命令来升级自己。
   616→
   617→**3. 包管理器生态（跨平台）**
   618→```bash
   619→brew upgrade gh         # macOS Homebrew
   620→scoop update gh         # Windows Scoop
   621→apt upgrade gh          # Linux apt
   622→```
   623→需要把包发布到各个包管理器。
   624→
   625→---
   626→
   627→**你们可以考虑的方案：**
   628→
   629→1. **短期**：文档里推荐 `npm update -g @openmnemo/cli`（比 install 短）
   630→
   631→2. **中期**：加一个 `openmnemo upgrade` 命令（内部执行 `npm install -g @openmnemo/cli@latest`），类似 `gh upgrade` 的做法
   632→
   633→3. **长期**：发布到 Homebrew/Scoop，用户可以 `brew upgrade openmnemo`
   634→
   635→大部分用户习惯了 npm 的长命令，但内置 `upgrade` 命令确实体验更好。像 `gh`、`turbo`、`vercel` 这些高频 CLI 都有自己的升级命令。

   647→### 62. assistant
   648→- Timestamp: `2026-03-18T12:11:47Z`
   649→
   650→现有的 `openmnemo upgrade` 命令是用来**升级项目配置**的（把仓库升级到 MemoryTree 结构），不是升级 CLI 工具本身。
   651→
   652→如果要用 CLI 自己的命令来升级，需要加一个新命令，比如：
   653→- `openmnemo self-update` 
   654→- `openmnemo cli-upgrade`
   655→- 或者在 `upgrade` 下加子命令 `openmnemo upgrade cli`
   656→
   657→但这样会有语义混淆（upgrade 既指升级项目，又指升级工具）。
   658→
   659→---
   660→
   661→**最实际的方案：**
   662→
   663→既然你们已经有 `upgrade` 命令了，最简单的升级 CLI 方式就是：
   664→
   665→```bash
   666→npm update -g @openmnemo/cli
   667→```
   668→
   669→或者在文档/README 里提供一个 shell 函数：
   670→
   671→```bash
   672→# 加到 ~/.bashrc 或 ~/.zshrc
   673→alias openmnemo-update='npm update -g @openmnemo/cli'
   674→```
   675→
   676→这样用户就可以 `openmnemo-update` 一键升级。
   677→
   678→大部分 CLI 工具（firebase、vercel、netlify）都是这么做的，用户也习惯了。只有像 `gh`、`rustup` 这种"工具链管理器"才会内置自升级命令。

   687→
   688→**回答你的三个问题：**
   689→
   690→## 1. 重新执行安装命令能升级吗？
   691→
   692→**能！** 这就是标准升级方式：
   693→
   694→```bash
   695→npm install -g @openmnemo/cli
   696→```
   697→
   698→重新执行这个命令，npm 会自动安装最新版，覆盖旧版。这就是升级。
   699→
   700→---
   701→
   702→## 2. 能用 `openmnemo update` 来升级 CLI 自己吗？
   703→
   704→**完全可以！** 技术上很简单，在 CLI 里加一个命令：
   705→
   706→```typescript
   707→program
   708→  .command('update')
   709→  .alias('u')
   710→  .description('Update openmnemo CLI to the latest version')
   711→  .action(() => {
   712→    execSync('npm install -g @openmnemo/cli@latest', { stdio: 'inherit' })
   713→  })
   714→```
   715→
   716→这样用户就可以 `openmnemo update` 或 `openmnemo u` 来升级。
   717→
   718→**但你们现在有个命名冲突：**
   719→- `upgrade` 已经被占用（升级项目配置到 MemoryTree）
   720→- 可以用 `update` 来升级 CLI 自己
   721→- 或者用 `self-update`、`cli-update`
   722→
   723→---
   724→
   725→## 3. 主流工具都这样做吗？
   726→
   727→**分两派：**
   728→
   729→### 有内置升级命令的（少数）：
   730→- `gh upgrade` - GitHub CLI
   731→- `rustup update` - Rust
   732→- `npm install -g npm` - npm 自己
   733→- `pnpm add -g pnpm` - pnpm 自己
   734→
   735→### 没有内置升级命令的（多数）：
   736→- `firebase-tools` → `npm install -g firebase-tools`
   737→- `vercel` → `npm install -g vercel`
   738→- `netlify-cli` → `npm install -g netlify-cli`
   739→- `typescript` → `npm install -g typescript`
   740→- `turbo` → `npm install -g turbo`
   741→
   742→**大部分 Node.js CLI 都没有内置升级命令**，直接让用户重新执行安装命令。
   743→
   744→---
   745→
   746→## 建议
   747→
   748→你们可以：
   749→
   750→1. **简单方案**：文档里写 `npm install -g @openmnemo/cli`（重新安装=升级）
   751→
   752→2. **友好方案**：加一个 `openmnemo update` 命令（内部调用 npm），用户体验更好
   753→
   754→3. **命名方案**：
   755→   - `openmnemo upgrade` - 升级项目配置（现有）
   756→   - `openmnemo update` - 升级 CLI 工具（新增）
   757→   - 或者 `openmnemo self-update`
   758→
   759→像 `gh` 这种高频工具有内置升级命令确实更方便，但不是必须的。

assistant #245 23:27:27

原始 jsonl 里有 118 条 type: user 消息，但 clean 版本只有 17 条。这不是压缩导致的——raw 里根本没有 summary 类型的消息。

问题出在 clean 脚本的解析逻辑上。那118条 user 消息里，很多是 tool_result 类型（97条），比如用户批准/拒绝工具调用的反馈。clean 脚本在做确定性清洗时，把这些 tool_result 类型的 user 消息过滤掉了，只保留了有实际文字内容的用户输入。

所以回答你的问题：

1. 不是压缩导致的。Claude Code 的上下文压缩不会产生新的 session，session ID 始终是同一个 2a22e074。
2. 不是对话消失了。原始 jsonl 里 357 行、118 条 user 消息都完整保存着。
3. 是 clean 脚本的过滤逻辑——它只提取了有实际文本内容的用户消息（17条），把 tool_result 反馈（批准/拒绝操作）都过滤掉了。

那些 subagent 文件（4个 agent-*.jsonl）也是同一个 session 里派生出来的子任务，不是新对话。

所以对话是连贯的，数据没丢。只是 clean 版本做了精简，只保留了"人说的话"。如果你需要看完整的交互过程（包括工具批准/拒绝），需要看 raw jsonl。

1→/**
     2→ * Transcript parsing — client inference, dispatch, and format-specific parsers.
     3→ * Port of scripts/_transcript_parse.py
     4→ */
     5→
     6→import { readFileSync, statSync } from 'node:fs'
     7→import { basename, extname } from 'node:path'
     8→
     9→import type { Client, ParsedTranscript, TranscriptMessage, TranscriptToolEvent } from '../types/transcript.js'
    10→import { toPosixPath } from '../utils/path.js'
    11→import {
    12→  SKIP_BLOCK_TYPES,
    13→  TEXT_BLOCK_TYPES,
    14→  TOOL_RESULT_TYPES,
    15→  TOOL_USE_TYPES,
    16→  deduplicateMessages,
    17→  deduplicateToolEvents,
    18→  earliestTimestamp,
    19→  ensureDict,
    20→  ensureList,
    21→  extractGeminiText,
    22→  extractTextBlocks,
    23→  findFirstMappingWithKeys,

    31→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    32→// Client inference + dispatch
    33→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    34→
    35→export function inferClient(client: string, sourcePath: string): Client {
    36→  if (client !== 'auto') {
    37→    return client as Client
    38→  }
    39→  const normalized = toPosixPath(sourcePath).toLowerCase()
    40→  const fileName = basename(sourcePath).toLowerCase()
    41→  if (normalized.includes('/.codex/') || fileName.startsWith('rollout-')) {
    42→    return 'codex'
    43→  }
    44→  if (normalized.includes('/.claude/') || normalized.includes('/projects/')) {
    45→    return 'claude'
    46→  }
    47→  if (normalized.includes('/.gemini/') || normalized.includes('checkpoint')) {
    48→    return 'gemini'
    49→  }
    50→  if (fileName.startsWith('doubao_') || normalized.includes('/doubao/')) {
    51→    return 'doubao'
    52→  }
    53→  throw new Error(`could not infer transcript client from source path: ${sourcePath}`)
    54→}
    55→
    56→export function parseTranscript(client: string, sourcePath: string): ParsedTranscript {
    57→  const resolved = inferClient(client, sourcePath)
    58→  if (resolved === 'codex') {
    59→    return parseCodexTranscript(sourcePath)
    60→  }
    61→  if (resolved === 'claude') {
    62→    return parseClaudeTranscript(sourcePath)
    63→  }
    64→  if (resolved === 'gemini') {
    65→    return parseGeminiTranscript(sourcePath)
    66→  }
    67→  if (resolved === 'doubao') {
    68→    return parseDoubaoTranscript(sourcePath)
    69→  }
    70→  throw new Error(`unsupported transcript client: ${resolved}`)
    71→}
    72→
    73→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    74→// Codex parser
    75→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    76→
    77→export function parseCodexTranscript(filePath: string): ParsedTranscript {
    78→  const records = loadJsonl(filePath)
    79→  const stem = basename(filePath, extname(filePath))
    80→  let sessionId = stem
    81→  let title = stem
    82→  let startedAt = normalizeTimestamp(statSync(filePath).mtimeMs / 1000)
    83→  let cwd = ''
    84→  let branch = ''
    85→  // Canonical messages from `payload.type === 'message'` (response_item records).
    86→  const messages: TranscriptMessage[] = []
    87→  // Streaming fallback: `agent_message` / `user_message` from event_msg records.
    88→  // The Codex CLI double-encodes every message: each turn fires as a streaming
    89→  // `event_msg` (agent_message / user_message) AND later as a canonical
    90→  // `response_item` (message). Processing both causes duplicates because the two
    91→  // representations share almost-identical but not always equal timestamps
    92→  // (millisecond jitter), defeating timestamp-based deduplication. We therefore
    93→  // prefer canonical records and use streaming records only as a fallback for
    94→  // sessions recorded by older Codex versions that emit only streaming events.
    95→  const streamingMessages: TranscriptMessage[] = []
    96→  const toolEvents: TranscriptToolEvent[] = []
    97→
    98→  for (const record of records) {
    99→    const recordType = String(record['type'] ?? '')
   100→    const timestamp = normalizeTimestamp(record['timestamp'], startedAt)
   101→
   102→    if (recordType === 'session_meta') {
   103→      const payload = ensureDict(record['payload'])
   104→      sessionId = String(payload['id'] ?? '') || sessionId
   105→      title = String(payload['thread_name'] ?? '') || String(payload['title'] ?? '') || title
   106→      startedAt = earliestTimestamp(startedAt, payload['timestamp'])
   107→      cwd = String(payload['cwd'] ?? '') || cwd
   108→      branch = String(getNested(payload, 'git', 'branch') ?? '') || branch
   109→      continue
   110→    }
   111→
   112→    if (recordType !== 'response_item' && recordType !== 'event_msg') {
   113→      continue
   114→    }
   115→
   116→    const payload = ensureDict(record['payload'])
   117→    const payloadType = String(payload['type'] ?? '')
   118→
   119→    if (payloadType === 'message') {
   120→      const role = String(payload['role'] ?? '').toLowerCase()
   121→      if (role === 'user' || role === 'assistant') {
   122→        const text = extractTextBlocks(payload['content'])
   123→        if (text) {
   124→          messages.push({ role, text, timestamp })
   125→        }
   126→      }
   127→      continue
   128→    }
   129→
   130→    // Collect streaming events as fallback only — never mix with canonical records.
   131→    if (payloadType === 'user_message' || payloadType === 'agent_message') {
   132→      const role = payloadType === 'user_message' ? 'user' : 'assistant'
   133→      const text = String(payload['message'] ?? '').trim()
   134→      if (text) {
   135→        streamingMessages.push({ role, text, timestamp })
   136→      }
   137→      continue
   138→    }
   139→
   140→    if (payloadType === 'function_call') {
   141→      const name = String(payload['name'] ?? '') || 'function_call'
   142→      const args = payload['arguments'] ?? payload['input']
   143→      toolEvents.push({
   144→        summary: `${name} input=${summarizeValue(args)}`,
   145→        timestamp,
   146→      })
   147→      continue
   148→    }
   149→
   150→    if (payloadType === 'custom_tool_call') {
   151→      const name = String(payload['name'] ?? '') || String(payload['call_id'] ?? '') || 'custom_tool_call'
   152→      toolEvents.push({
   153→        summary: `${name} input=${summarizeValue(payload['input'])}`,
   154→        timestamp,
   155→      })
   156→      continue
   157→    }
   158→
   159→    if (payloadType === 'function_call_output') {
   160→      const name = String(payload['name'] ?? '') || String(payload['call_id'] ?? '') || 'function_call_output'
   161→      const output = payload['output'] ?? payload['content']
   162→      toolEvents.push({
   163→        summary: `${name} output=${summarizeValue(output)}`,
   164→        timestamp,
   165→      })
   166→      continue
   167→    }
   168→
   169→    if (payloadType === 'custom_tool_call_output') {
   170→      const name = String(payload['name'] ?? '') || String(payload['call_id'] ?? '') || 'custom_tool_call_output'
   171→      const output = payload['output'] ?? payload['content']
   172→      toolEvents.push({
   173→        summary: `${name} output=${summarizeValue(output)}`,
   174→        timestamp,
   175→      })
   176→    }
   177→  }
   178→
   179→  // Use canonical records when available; fall back to streaming events otherwise.
   180→  // Then drop only the leading Codex system injection messages so we do not
   181→  // accidentally erase later turns where the user is legitimately discussing
   182→  // AGENTS.md, environment tags, or other injected scaffolding.
   183→  const finalMessages = trimLeadingCodexSystemInjections(
   184→    messages.length > 0 ? messages : streamingMessages,
   185→  )
   186→
   187→  return {
   188→    client: 'codex',
   189→    session_id: sessionId,
   190→    title,
   191→    started_at: startedAt,
   192→    cwd,
   193→    branch,
   194→    messages: deduplicateMessages(finalMessages),
   195→    tool_events: deduplicateToolEvents(toolEvents),
   196→    source_path: filePath,
   197→  }
   198→}
   199→
   200→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   201→// Codex system injection detection
   202→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   203→
   204→// The Codex CLI injects system context — AGENTS.md instructions, skill
   205→// definitions, environment metadata, and permissions — as the first
   206→// `message(role=user)` record of every session. These are not real user turns
   207→// and must be filtered so the clean transcript starts with the actual
   208→// conversation.
   209→const CODEX_INJECTION_MARKERS: readonly string[] = [
   210→  '<INSTRUCTIONS>',
   211→  '<environment_context>',
   212→  '<permissions instructions>',
   213→  '<collaboration_mode>',
   214→  '# AGENTS.md instructions for',
   215→]
   216→
   217→export function isCodexSystemInjection(text: string): boolean {
   218→  return CODEX_INJECTION_MARKERS.some(marker => text.includes(marker))
   219→}
   220→
   221→function trimLeadingCodexSystemInjections(messages: TranscriptMessage[]): TranscriptMessage[] {
   222→  let firstRealIndex = 0
   223→  while (firstRealIndex < messages.length) {
   224→    const message = messages[firstRealIndex]
   225→    if (!message || message.role !== 'user' || !isCodexSystemInjection(message.text)) {
   226→      break
   227→    }
   228→    firstRealIndex++
   229→  }
   230→  return messages.slice(firstRealIndex)
   231→}
   232→
   233→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   234→// Claude parser
   235→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   236→
   237→export function parseClaudeTranscript(filePath: string): ParsedTranscript {
   238→  const records = loadJsonl(filePath)
   239→  const stem = basename(filePath, extname(filePath))
   240→  let sessionId = stem
   241→  const title = stem
   242→  let startedAt = normalizeTimestamp(statSync(filePath).mtimeMs / 1000)
   243→  let cwd = ''
   244→  let branch = ''
   245→  const messages: TranscriptMessage[] = []
   246→  const toolEvents: TranscriptToolEvent[] = []
   247→
   248→  for (const record of records) {
   249→    const recordType = String(record['type'] ?? '')
   250→    const timestamp = normalizeTimestamp(record['timestamp'], startedAt)
   251→    sessionId = String(record['sessionId'] ?? '') || sessionId
   252→    startedAt = earliestTimestamp(startedAt, record['timestamp'])
   253→    cwd = String(record['cwd'] ?? '') || cwd
   254→    branch = String(record['gitBranch'] ?? '') || branch
   255→
   256→    if (recordType !== 'user' && recordType !== 'assistant') {
   257→      continue
   258→    }
   259→
   260→    const message = ensureDict(record['message'])
   261→    const role = String(message['role'] ?? '').toLowerCase() || recordType
   262→    const textParts: string[] = []
   263→    const content = message['content']
   264→
   265→    if (typeof content === 'string') {
   266→      const text = content.trim()
   267→      if ((role === 'user' || role === 'assistant') && text) {
   268→        messages.push({ role, text, timestamp })
   269→      }
   270→      continue
   271→    }
   272→
   273→    for (const block of ensureList(content)) {
   274→      if (typeof block === 'string') {
   275→        if (block.trim()) {
   276→          textParts.push(block.trim())
   277→        }
   278→        continue
   279→      }
   280→      if (block === null || typeof block !== 'object' || Array.isArray(block)) {
   281→        continue
   282→      }
   283→      const rec = block as Record<string, unknown>
   284→      const blockType = String(rec['type'] ?? '').toLowerCase()
   285→
   286→      if (TEXT_BLOCK_TYPES.has(blockType)) {
   287→        const text = String(rec['text'] ?? '').trim()
   288→        if (text) {
   289→          textParts.push(text)
   290→        }
   291→        continue
   292→      }
   293→      if (SKIP_BLOCK_TYPES.has(blockType)) {
   294→        continue
   295→      }
   296→      if (TOOL_USE_TYPES.has(blockType)) {
   297→        const name = String(rec['name'] ?? '') || 'tool_use'
   298→        toolEvents.push({
   299→          summary: `${name} input=${summarizeValue(rec['input'])}`,
   300→          timestamp,
   301→        })
   302→        continue
   303→      }
   304→      if (TOOL_RESULT_TYPES.has(blockType)) {
   305→        const toolUseId = String(rec['tool_use_id'] ?? '') || 'tool_result'
   306→        toolEvents.push({
   307→          summary: `${toolUseId} output=${summarizeValue(rec['content'])}`,
   308→          timestamp,
   309→        })
   310→      }
   311→    }
   312→
   313→    const text = joinParagraphs(textParts)
   314→    if ((role === 'user' || role === 'assistant') && text) {
   315→      messages.push({ role, text, timestamp })
   316→    }
   317→  }
   318→
   319→  return {
   320→    client: 'claude',
   321→    session_id: sessionId,
   322→    title,
   323→    started_at: startedAt,
   324→    cwd,
   325→    branch,
   326→    messages: deduplicateMessages(messages),
   327→    tool_events: deduplicateToolEvents(toolEvents),
   328→    source_path: filePath,
   329→  }
   330→}
   331→
   332→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   333→// Gemini parser
   334→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   335→
   336→export function parseGeminiTranscript(filePath: string): ParsedTranscript {
   337→  const stem = basename(filePath, extname(filePath))
   338→  let sessionId = stem
   339→  const title = stem
   340→  let startedAt = normalizeTimestamp(statSync(filePath).mtimeMs / 1000)
   341→  let cwd = ''
   342→  let branch = ''
   343→  const messages: TranscriptMessage[] = []
   344→  const toolEvents: TranscriptToolEvent[] = []
   345→
   346→  let payload: unknown
   347→  if (extname(filePath).toLowerCase() === '.jsonl') {
   348→    payload = loadJsonl(filePath)
   349→  } else {
   350→    payload = JSON.parse(readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8')) as unknown
   351→  }
   352→
   353→  const metaKeys: ReadonlySet<string> = new Set(['sessionId', 'chatId', 'cwd', 'branch', 'timestamp'])
   354→  const firstMeta = findFirstMappingWithKeys(payload, metaKeys)
   355→  if (firstMeta !== null) {
   356→    sessionId = String(firstMeta['sessionId'] ?? '') || String(firstMeta['chatId'] ?? '') || String(firstMeta['id'] ?? '') || sessionId
   357→    startedAt = earliestTimestamp(startedAt, firstMeta['timestamp'])
   358→    cwd = String(firstMeta['cwd'] ?? '') || String(firstMeta['projectRoot'] ?? '') || cwd
   359→    branch = String(firstMeta['branch'] ?? '') || branch
   360→  }
   361→
   362→  function visit(node: unknown): void {
   363→    if (Array.isArray(node)) {
   364→      for (const item of node) {
   365→        visit(item)
   366→      }
   367→      return
   368→    }
   369→    if (node === null || typeof node !== 'object') {
   370→      return
   371→    }
   372→    const rec = node as Record<string, unknown>
   373→
   374→    sessionId = String(rec['sessionId'] ?? '') || String(rec['chatId'] ?? '') || String(rec['id'] ?? '') || sessionId
   375→    startedAt = earliestTimestamp(startedAt, rec['timestamp'])
   376→    cwd = String(rec['cwd'] ?? '') || String(rec['projectRoot'] ?? '') || cwd
   377→    branch = String(rec['branch'] ?? '') || branch
   378→
   379→    const role = String(rec['role'] ?? rec['author'] ?? rec['sender'] ?? '').toLowerCase()
   380→    const timestamp = normalizeTimestamp(rec['timestamp'], startedAt)
   381→
   382→    if (role === 'user' || role === 'assistant' || role === 'model') {
   383→      const normalizedRole = role === 'model' ? 'assistant' : role
   384→      const text = extractGeminiText(rec)
   385→      if (text) {
   386→        messages.push({ role: normalizedRole, text, timestamp })
   387→      }
   388→    }
   389→
   390→    const toolName =
   391→      getNested(rec, 'toolUse', 'name') ??
   392→      rec['toolName'] ??
   393→      rec['functionName'] ??
   394→      rec['tool']
   395→    if (toolName) {
   396→      toolEvents.push({
   397→        summary: `${String(toolName)} input=${summarizeValue(rec['args'] ?? rec['input'])}`,
   398→        timestamp,
   399→      })
   400→    }
   401→
   402→    for (const value of Object.values(rec)) {
   403→      visit(value)
   404→    }
   405→  }
   406→
   407→  visit(payload)
   408→
   409→  return {
   410→    client: 'gemini',
   411→    session_id: sessionId,
   412→    title,
   413→    started_at: startedAt,
   414→    cwd,
   415→    branch,
   416→    messages: deduplicateMessages(messages),
   417→    tool_events: deduplicateToolEvents(toolEvents),
   418→    source_path: filePath,
   419→  }
   420→}
   421→
   422→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   423→// Doubao parser
   424→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   425→//
   426→// Doubao TXT export format:
   427→//
   428→//   Title: 对话标题
   429→//   URL: https://www.doubao.com/chat/38416801786598914
   430→//   Platform: 豆包
   431→//   Created: 2026-03-16 10:22:17
   432→//   Messages: 28
   433→//
   434→//   User: [2026-03-16 10:22:17]
   435→//   用户消息内容...
   436→//
   437→//   AI: [2026-03-16 15:43:17]
   438→//   AI 回复内容...
   439→//
   440→
   441→/** Matches a turn header: "User: [2026-03-16 10:22:17]" or "AI: [2026-03-16 15:43:17]" */
   442→const DOUBAO_TURN_RE = /^(User|AI):\s*\[(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}\s+\d{2}:\d{2}:\d{2})\]\s*$/
   443→
   444→export function parseDoubaoTranscript(filePath: string): ParsedTranscript {
   445→  const content = readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8')
   446→  const lines = content.split('\n')
   447→
   448→  const stem = basename(filePath, extname(filePath))
   449→  let title = stem
   450→  let sessionId = stem
   451→  let startedAt = normalizeTimestamp(statSync(filePath).mtimeMs / 1000)
   452→
   453→  // --- Parse header block (key: value lines before the first blank line) ---
   454→  let lineIndex = 0
   455→  for (; lineIndex < lines.length; lineIndex++) {
   456→    const line = lines[lineIndex] ?? ''
   457→    if (line.trim() === '') break
   458→
   459→    const titleMatch = line.match(/^Title:\s*(.+)$/)
   460→    if (titleMatch) {
   461→      title = (titleMatch[1] ?? '').trim() || title
   462→      continue
   463→    }
   464→
   465→    const urlMatch = line.match(/^URL:\s*(.+)$/)
   466→    if (urlMatch) {
   467→      const url = (urlMatch[1] ?? '').trim()
   468→      // Derive session_id from the last path segment of the URL
   469→      const lastSegment = url.split('/').pop() ?? ''
   470→      if (lastSegment) sessionId = lastSegment
   471→      continue
   472→    }
   473→
   474→    const createdMatch = line.match(/^Created:\s*(.+)$/)
   475→    if (createdMatch) {
   476→      // Doubao exports user-local time with no timezone info.
   477→      // Convert "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS" → "YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SS" (naive, no Z suffix)
   478→      // so we don't falsely claim UTC.
   479→      const raw = (createdMatch[1] ?? '').trim().replace(' ', 'T')
   480→      if (raw) startedAt = raw
   481→      continue
   482→    }
   483→  }
   484→
   485→  // Skip blank lines between header and first turn
   486→  while (lineIndex < lines.length && (lines[lineIndex] ?? '').trim() === '') {
   487→    lineIndex++
   488→  }
   489→
   490→  // --- Parse message turns ---
   491→  const messages: TranscriptMessage[] = []
   492→
   493→  while (lineIndex < lines.length) {
   494→    const line = lines[lineIndex] ?? ''
   495→    const match = line.match(DOUBAO_TURN_RE)
   496→
   497→    if (!match) {
   498→      lineIndex++
   499→      continue
   500→    }
   501→
   502→    const role: string = match[1] === 'User' ? 'user' : 'assistant'
   503→    // Doubao exports user-local time — keep as naive ISO, no Z suffix.
   504→    const timestamp = (match[2] ?? '').trim().replace(' ', 'T')
   505→    lineIndex++ // advance past turn header
   506→
   507→    // Skip blank line that follows the turn header
   508→    while (lineIndex < lines.length && (lines[lineIndex] ?? '').trim() === '') {
   509→      lineIndex++
   510→    }
   511→
   512→    // Collect body lines until next turn header or EOF
   513→    const bodyLines: string[] = []
   514→    while (lineIndex < lines.length) {
   515→      const bodyLine = lines[lineIndex] ?? ''
   516→      if (DOUBAO_TURN_RE.test(bodyLine)) break
   517→      bodyLines.push(bodyLine)
   518→      lineIndex++
   519→    }
   520→
   521→    // Trim trailing blank lines from body
   522→    while (bodyLines.length > 0 && (bodyLines[bodyLines.length - 1] ?? '').trim() === '') {
   523→      bodyLines.pop()
   524→    }
   525→
   526→    const text = bodyLines.join('\n').trim()
   527→    if (text) {
   528→      messages.push({ role, text, timestamp })
   529→    }
   530→  }
   531→
   532→  return {
   533→    client: 'doubao',
   534→    session_id: sessionId,
   535→    title,
   536→    started_at: startedAt,
   537→    cwd: '',
   538→    branch: '',
   539→    messages: deduplicateMessages(messages),
   540→    tool_events: [],
   541→    source_path: filePath,
   542→  }
   543→}
   544→
assistant #250 23:36:13

找到原因了。看 Claude parser（第256行）：

if (recordType !== 'user' && recordType !== 'assistant') {
  continue
}

它只处理 type: "user" 和 type: "assistant" 的记录。但之前我们看到 raw jsonl 里的 type 分布：

- user: 118 条
- assistant: 151 条
- message: 151 条
- progress: 86 条
- tool_result: 97 条
- 等等

parser 确实进入了 118 条 user 记录。但关键在第 262-316 行：它遍历每条 user 记录的 message.content 数组，只提取 TEXT_BLOCK_TYPES（文本块），而 TOOL_RESULT_TYPES 被归入 toolEvents，SKIP_BLOCK_TYPES 直接跳过。

也就是说，118 条 type: "user" 记录里，大部分的 content 只包含 tool_result 块（用户批准/拒绝工具调用的反馈），没有实际文字内容。第 313-316 行：

const text = joinParagraphs(textParts)
if ((role === 'user' || role === 'assistant') && text) {
  messages.push({ role, text, timestamp })
}

只有 text 非空才会被保留为消息。所以 118 条 user 记录中，只有 17 条包含了你实际打字输入的文本，其余 101 条都是纯 tool_result（批准工具执行），没有文字内容，被过滤掉了。

这不是 bug，是设计如此——clean 版本只保留有实际文字的对话，工具交互记录放在了 Tool Events 区域。对话也没有因为压缩而断裂，session ID 始终是同一个 2a22e074，357 行原始数据完整保存在 raw jsonl 里。
